)@@G@@(@EDM) IS A PROGRAM     @G@@@@ DESIGNED  TO  EDIT  PROGRAMS  AND/OR DATAKX

)@@G@@ITY AND POWER.   ALTHOUGH     @G@@@@ THE  EDITOR  CAN  BE  USED WITH ONLLC
)@@G@@Y KNOWLEDGE OF THE BASIC SET OF     @G@@@@ COMMANDS, THE MORE SOPHISTICALD
)@@G@@TED COMMANDS ALLOW MANY EDITING TASKS     @G@@@@ TO  BE  DONE MUCH MORE LE
)@@G@@RAPIDLY.   THE MORE ADVANCED COMMANDS ALLOW     @G@@@@ FOR  SELECTIVELY LF
)@@G@@ PRINTING  RESULTS  (CUTTING  DOWN  ON TIME SPENT     @G@@@@ WAITING  FOLG
)@@G@@R  TERMINAL PRINTOUT),  DOING SEVERAL OF THE BASIC COM-     @G@@@@ MANDSLH
)@@G@@ IN ONE STEP,  ALIGNING COLUMNS WITH A TAB FEATURE, MANIPULA-     @B@@@@LI
)@@G@@ TING GROUPS OF IMAGES AS A UNIT, ETC.    @[@@@@      @G@@@@       THIS LJ
)@@G@@ EDITOR  IS  UNDER  CONTINUOUS  DEVELOPMENT  BY THE UOM     @G@@@@ SYSTELK
)@@G@@M'S STAFF.   ITS IMMEDIATE ANCESTOR WAS LEVEL 9 OF THE UNIVAC     @G@@@@LL
)@@G@@ @EDM  PROCESSOR  WHICH WAS IN TURN DERIVED FROM J.  SALZER'S 'CTSS'    LM
)@@G@@@G@@@@ EDITOR  WRITTEN AT MIT.   SINCE WE HAVE NO SCRUPLES,  A GREAT MANLN
)@@G@@Y     @G@@@@ NIFTY  FEATURES  WERE  PIRATED  FROM  OTHER  EDITORS SUCH ALO
)@@G@@S THOSE     @G@@@@ AVAILABLE  ON  GE  AND  DEC SYSTEMS.   THE    MATCH  LP
)@@G@@  COMMAND WAS     @G@@@@ ORIGINALLY DESIGNED AND IMPLEMENTED AT THE UNIVLQ
)@@G@@ERSITY OF WISCONSIN     @G@@@@ BY ERIC NORMAN.  MANY OTHER USEFUL IDEAS LR
)@@G@@AND SUGGESTIONS WERE MADE     @G@@@@ BY  THE  UOM USER COMMUNITY,  BUT MLS

)@@G@@S EFFORTS.  @[@@@@      @G@@@@       USERS ARE CAUTIONED THAT ALTHOUGH TLU
)@@G@@HE UOM EDITOR WAS DERIVED     @G@@@@ FROM  A  UNIVAC  EDITOR,   IT IS NOLV

)@@G@@NCES FOR THE UOM EDITOR.   DIFFERENCES FROM     @C@@@@ THE UNIVAC EDITORLY
)@@G@@ ARE TABULATED IN AN APPENDIX.@[@@@@      @G@@@@       THIS  VERSION  OFLZ

)@@G@@LE  IN  LEVEL 28 OF THE UOM EDITOR.   IT IS BEING     @G@@@@ RELEASED PRMB

)@@G@@WINDOW AT ANY GIVEN TIME IS THE     @G@@@@ 'CURRENT' LINE.   IT IS POSSINE
)@@G@@BLE FOR THE WINDOW TO BE EMPTY; DELE-     @F@@@@ TING THE CURRENT LINE, NF

)@@G@@S OR DONE A   TOP   AND THE WINDOW IS     @]@@@@ EMPTY,     @[@@@@      SY

)@@G@@@[@@@@      @[@@@@      @^@@@@ 11.   ASCII EDITING    @[@@@@      @[@@@@FC
)@@G@@      @[@@@@      @[@@@@      @[@@@@      @#@@@@ 11. 1.   GENERAL @[@@@@FD
)@@G@@      @[@@@@      @G@@@@       THE UOM  @EDM  PROCESSOR ENABLES THE USERFE
)@@G@@ TO EDIT FULL ASCII     @G@@@@ FILES  REGARDLESS  OF  WHETHER  THE  TERMFF
)@@G@@INAL  BEING USED HAS FULL     @G@@@@ UPPER-LOWER  CASE  CAPABILITY  OR  FG
)@@G@@NOT.    TWO OPTIONS ARE USED TO     @G@@@@ CONTROL  THE CODES USED (FIELFH
)@@G@@DATA OR ASCII),  THEY ARE    P    AND     @]@@@@ Q    .     @[@@@@      FI
)@@G@@@G@@@@       THE  Q-OPTION CONDITIONS THE EDITOR TO ACCEPT BOTH UPPER ANFJ
)@@G@@D     @G@@@@ LOWER  CASE INPUT,  WHILE NO Q-OPTION INDICATES THE TERMINAFK
)@@G@@L INPUT     @G@@@@ IS  TO BE TREATED AS MONOCASE.   NOTE THAT IF THE EDIFL
)@@G@@TOR IS IN THE     @G@@@@ MONOCASE MODE,  INPUT FROM A TERMINAL WILL BE 'FM
)@@G@@FOLDED' (SEE BELOW)     @G@@@@ ONTO  THE  FIELDATA  SET  EVEN IF THE TERFN
)@@G@@MINAL ITSELF CAN GENERATE     @ @@@@ BOTH UPPER AND LOWER CASE.   @[@@@@FO
)@@G@@      @G@@@@       NORMALLY,   THE  FINAL OUTPUT OF THE EDITOR WILL BE TFP
)@@G@@HE SAME     @G@@@@ MODE  AS  THAT  OF  THE  TERMINAL,  E.G.   IF THE Q-OFQ
)@@G@@PTION IS USED     @G@@@@ (INDICATING  THAT  THE  TERMINAL  HAS UPPER-LOWFR
)@@G@@ER CASE) THE OUTPUT     @G@@@@ WOULD BE UPPER AND LOWER CASE FULL ASCII.FS
)@@G@@   THE P-OPTION INDICATES     @G@@@@ THAT  A  CODE TRANSLATION OF THE OUFT
)@@G@@TPUT ELEMENT SHOULD TAKE PLACE.     @]@@@@ FOR EXAMPLE@[@@@@      @ @@@@FU
)@@G@@                   @EDM,P     @[@@@@      @G@@@@ INDICATES THAT THE TERMFV
)@@G@@INAL IS MONOCASE,  BUT THE OUTPUT SHOULD BE     @A@@@@ TRANSLATED TO FULFW
)@@G@@L ASCII, WHILE    @[@@@@      @ @@@@                   @EDM,QP    @[@@@@FX
)@@G@@      @G@@@@ INDICATES  THAT  THE  TERMINAL  MAY  GENERATE BOTH UPPER ANFY
)@@G@@D LOWER     @B@@@@ CASE, BUT THE OUTPUT SHOULD BE FIELDATA. @[@@@@      FZ
)@@G@@@[@@@@      @ @@@@ 11. 2.   CODE TRANSLATION    @[@@@@      @[@@@@      GA
)@@G@@@G@@@@       REGARDLESS  OF THE CODE OF THE FINAL EDITOR OUTPUT,  EDITINGB
)@@G@@G     @G@@@@ TAKES  PLACE IN THE CODE SPECIFIED BY THE TERMINAL,  I.E.  GC
)@@G@@ IF THE     @G@@@@ TERMINAL  IS  MONOCASE,   EDITING TAKES PLACE IN FIELGD
)@@G@@DATA;  IF THE     @G@@@@ TERMINAL  IS FULL ASCII,  EDITING TAKES PLACE IGE
)@@G@@N FULL ASCII.   THE     @G@@@@ EDITOR  AUTOMATICALLY  TAKES  CARE  OF  CGF

)@@G@@D ELEMENTS  @[@@@@      @[@@@@      @G@@@@       THE  EXEC  8 SYSTEM PRONG
)@@G@@VIDES TWO BASIC KINDS OF FILES,  DATA     @G@@@@ FILES AND PROGRAM FILESNH

)@@G@@MAT) FILES PRODUCED BY THE    @DATA PROCES-     @G@@@@ SOR,     PRINT$  NM
)@@G@@  FILES PRODUCED BY    @BRKPT , AND FILES WRITTEN     @G@@@@ WITH FORTRANN
)@@G@@N FORMATTED OUTPUT STATEMENTS.   SINCE A DATA FILE IS A     @G@@@@ CONTINO
)@@G@@NOUS  SEQUENCE  OF IMAGES (POSSIBLY INTERSPERSED WITH CONTROL     @G@@@@NP
)@@G@@ INFORMATION  DEPENDING  ON  FILE TYPE),  ONE OBTAINS ACCESS TO THE     NQ
)@@G@@@D@@@@ CONTENTS OF THE FILE MERELY BY SPECIFYING ITS NAME.  @[@@@@      NR
)@@G@@@G@@@@       PROGRAM  FILES CAN,  IN A SENSE,  BE CONSIDERED TO BE 'SUPENS
)@@G@@R     @G@@@@ FILES'.   A  PROGRAM  FILE MAY CONTAIN NOT JUST ONE SET OF NT
)@@G@@IMAGES,     @G@@@@ BUT  MANY,  AND EACH SET OF IMAGES IS INDIVIDUALLY NANU
)@@G@@MED.   IF THE     @G@@@@ SO-CALLED  'ELEMENTS'  OF  SUCH  A  FILE  ARE  NV

)@@G@@FACT,  THE FORMAT OF A SYMBOLIC     @G@@@@ ELEMENT WITHIN A PROGRAM FILENY
)@@G@@ IS NEARLY IDENTICAL TO THE FORMAT OF     @G@@@@ AN  SDF FORMAT FILE.   NZ
)@@G@@IT IS IN THIS SENSE THAT A PROGRAM FILE MAY     @G@@@@ BE  VIEWED AS A 'OA
)@@G@@SUPER FILE';  A PROGRAM FILE CAN BE CONSIDERED TO     @G@@@@ BE  A  COLLOB
)@@G@@ECTION OF INDIVIDUAL SYMBOLIC DATA FILES,  EACH INDIVI-     @G@@@@ DUALLOC
)@@G@@Y NAMED.  OBVIOUSLY, THEN, WHEN ONE WISHES TO REFER TO A DECK     @G@@@@OD
)@@G@@ IN A PROGRAM FILE,  ONE MUST SPECIFY BOTH THE NAME OF THE FILE AND     OE
)@@G@@@C@@@@ THE NAME OF THE DECK (ELEMENT) WITHIN THE FILE.@[@@@@      @G@@@@OF

)@@G@@A     @F@@@@ PROGRAM FILE MAY BE RELOCATABLE PROGRAM DECKS OR ABSOLUTE POI
)@@G@@RO-   @G@@@@ GRAMS,   IN ADDITION TO SYMBOLIC TEXT.   EACH ELEMENT IN A OJ

)@@G@@AME PROGRAM FILE.   SINCE     @G@@@@ THE  EDITOR ONLY OPERATES ON SYMBOLON

)@@G@@HAR ) @^@@@@      NCHAR=NCHAR + 1   @]@@@@      RETURN@]@@@@      END   FP
)@@G@@___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@^@@@@      SUBROUTINE PRTLN  @[@@@@FQ
)@@G@@C     @A@@@@C  PRINT LINE S/R. NCHAR CHARACTERS @[@@@@C     @B@@@@      FR
)@@G@@COMMON /IMAGE/ BLANK,NCHAR,LINE(22) @#@@@@      N=NCHAR/6   @A@@@@      FS
)@@G@@IF ( 6*N.NE.NCHAR )N=N + 1    @^@@@@      ERPRINT 1,N,LINE  @]@@@@      FT
)@@G@@RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@@FU
)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@^@@@@          AXR$      .   @]@@@@$(1)      . @[@@@@.     FV
)@@G@@@B@@@@.         CALL BTOCT ( NUMBER,OCTAL )     @[@@@@.     @C@@@@.     FW

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE GROUP(BUF,N1,N2,LIM,DEL,STR,N,LOC)   @ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTHC

)@@G@@TURN  @]@@@@$(0)      . @ @@@@SPACES    '            ' .    @B@@@@SAVE  MT
)@@G@@    RES      5                  .   @#@@@@          END     ___ RES     MU
)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@B@@@@      SUBROUTINE DMPIT ( NI,ID,NB,BLK )   @[@@@@C     MV
)@@G@@@C@@@@C  DUMP BLOCK - NB WORDS OF BLK  NI WORDS OF ID.@[@@@@C     @ @@@@MW
)@@G@@      COMMON /CONV/ NUM,NUMFD @B@@@@      COMMON /IMAGE/ BLANK,NCHAR,LINMX
)@@G@@E(22) @ @@@@      DIMENSION ID(2),BLK(2)  @[@@@@C     @ @@@@      IF ( NMY
)@@G@@B.LE.0 )GO TO 33  @^@@@@      ERPRINT 1,NI,ID   @#@@@@      CALL CLRLN  MZ
)@@G@@@#@@@@      DO 22 I=1,NB@A@@@@      CALL BTOCT ( BLK(I),NUMFD )   @ @@@@NA
)@@G@@      CALL INSTWO ( NUMFD )   @ @@@@      CALL INCHAR ( BLANK )   @ @@@@NB
)@@G@@      IF ( I.EQ.NB )GO TO 11  @A@@@@      IF ( NCHAR.LT.50 )GO TO 22    NC
)@@G@@@#@@@@   11 CALL PRTLN  @#@@@@      CALL CLRLN  @#@@@@   22 CONTINUE    ND
)@@G@@@]@@@@   33 RETURN@]@@@@      END   ___^=T/%0^=V/%0^=X/%0^=Z/%0^=-/%0^=$NE
)@@G@@/%0^$8/%0^=*9(@^*Q/K@^=*9(@^[O/K@^=*[[@^*W/K@^=*[[@^*S/K@^=*[[@^*U/K@^=*NF
)@@G@@9(G@@]%80@@./K@^=*9!@^!P9(@^!-/K@^=*9(G@@AR#K@[ *[@@@@*SDFF*@]@@@@COMM* NG

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE ELCHK ( CURSEQ,$ ) @[@@@@C     @#@@@@C  CHECK ELEMENT  @D@@@@RP

)@@G@@STAT=S1( FIO1(4) )@]@@@@      NERR=0@#@@@@      GO TO 233   @[@@@@C     SH
)@@G@@@F@@@@C  SYMBOLIC ELEMENT - CHECK CONTROL WORDS,IMAGE LENGTH, AND EOF   SI

)@@G@@*[@@@@*SDFF*@^@@@@      SUBROUTINE ERSYM  @[@@@@C     @^@@@@C  ELEMENT RTO

)@@G@@SUBROUTINE EQUATE ( NSPEC,TYPE,EXC,FASG,FAC )   @^@@@@      ASM$INTERFACBO
)@@G@@E 35-0@ @@@@      IMPLICIT INTEGER (A-Z)  @[@@@@C     @^@@@@C     NSPEC=BP
)@@G@@SPEC. NO.   @ @@@@C     TYPE=1 FASTRAND ONLY    @^@@@@C         =2 TAPE BQ
)@@G@@ONLY  @^@@@@C         =3 EITHER     @B@@@@C  EXC=0 ASSIGN (NOT EXCLUSIVEBR
)@@G@@) A OPTION  @B@@@@C     =1 ASSIGN (EXCLUSIVE) AX OPTION     @C@@@@C FASGBS
)@@G@@=0 ALREADY ASSIGNED WHEN PROCESSOR CALLED @ @@@@C     =1 DYNAMIC ASSIGNEBT
)@@G@@D.    @E@@@@C     FAC=FACILITY PACKET (WITH INTERNAL FILE NAME WANTED)  BU
)@@G@@@[@@@@C     @ @@@@      COMMON /CONV/ NUM,NUMFD @B@@@@      COMMON /IMAGBV
)@@G@@E/ BLANK,NCHAR,LINE(22) @^@@@@      DIMENSION FAC(10) @^@@@@      DIMENSBW
)@@G@@ION MSG(4)  @D@@@@      DATA MSG/ 'NOT#FASTRAND' , 'NOT#TAPE.   ' /     BX
)@@G@@@B@@@@      ARGUMENT FACIT$ ( L/A0/ , C/ER/ )   @B@@@@      ARGUMENT CSFBY
)@@G@@$ ( V/A0/ , C/ER/ )     @ @@@@      ARGUMENT ERR$ ( C/ER/ ) @[@@@@C     BZ
)@@G@@@^@@@@C  DO DUSE$ ON SPEC.    @[@@@@C     @ @@@@      STAT=INUSE( NSPEC,CA
)@@G@@FAC ) @ @@@@      IF ( STAT.GE.0 )GO TO 11@#@@@@      CALL CLRLN  @^@@@@CB
)@@G@@      LINE(1)='@USE E'  @^@@@@      LINE(2)='ERROR.'  @^@@@@      LINE(3CC
)@@G@@)=FAC(1)    @^@@@@  777 ERPRINT 1,10,LINE @#@@@@      CALL CLRLN  @A@@@@CD
)@@G@@      CALL INSTWO ( 'FAC#REJECT:#' )@A@@@@      CALL BTOCT ( STAT,NUMFD CE
)@@G@@)     @ @@@@      CALL INSTWO ( NUMFD )   @#@@@@      CALL PRTLN  @#@@@@CF
)@@G@@  999 CALL ERR$   @ @@@@   11 CALL FACIT$ ( FAC )     @^@@@@      IEQ=S1CG
)@@G@@( FAC(7) )  @]@@@@      FASG=0@ @@@@      IF ( IEQ.GT.0 )GO TO 33 @[@@@@CH
)@@G@@C     @A@@@@C  NOT ASSIGNED - DO DYNAMIC ASSIGN @[@@@@C     @]@@@@      CI
)@@G@@FASG=1@#@@@@      CALL CLRLN  @A@@@@      CALL INSONE ( '@ASG,A ' )     CJ
)@@G@@@C@@@@      IF ( EXC.GT.0 )CALL INCHAR ( '     X' )   @ @@@@      CALL ICK
)@@G@@NCHAR ( BLANK )   @ @@@@      CALL INSTWO ( FAC )     @ @@@@      CALL ICL
)@@G@@NSONE ( '.##.# ' )@B@@@@      CALL CSF$ ( 5*2**18+LOC(LINE) )     @ @@@@CM
)@@G@@      CALL REG$A0 ( STAT )    @A@@@@      IF ( STAT.LT.0 )GO TO 777     CN
)@@G@@@ @@@@      CALL FACIT$ ( FAC )     @^@@@@      IEQ=S1( FAC(7) )  @ @@@@CO
